# Test Report

Time: 2024-04-02 07:29:04.635289

### Base Program

```py
def validateBinaryTreeNodes(n, leftChild, rightChild):
    parent = [-1] * n
    for i in range(n):
        if leftChild[i] != -1:
            if parent[leftChild[i]] != -1:
                return False
            parent[leftChild[i]] = i
        if rightChild[i] != -1:
            if parent[rightChild[i]] != -1:
                return False
            parent[rightChild[i]] = i
    
    root = -1
    for i in range(n):
        if parent[i] == -1:
            if root != -1:
                return False
            root = i

    return root != -1
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py

def validateBinaryTreeNodes(n, leftChild, rightChild):
    parent = [-1] * n
    for i in range(n):
        if leftChild[i] != -1:
            if parent[leftChild[i]] != -1:
                return False
            parent[leftChild[i]] = i
        if rightChild[i] != -1:
            if parent[rightChild[i]] != -1:
                return False
            parent[rightChild[i]] = i
    
    root = -1
    for i in range(n):
        if parent[i] == -1:
            if root != -1:
                return False
            root = i

    return root != -1
```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py

def validateBinaryTreeNodes(n, leftChild, rightChild):
    parent = [-1] * n
    for i in range(n):
        if leftChild[i] != -1:
            if parent[leftChild[i]] != -1:
                return False
            parent[leftChild[i]] = i
        if rightChild[i] != -1:
            if parent[rightChild[i]] != -1:
                return False
            parent[rightChild[i]] = i
    
    root = -1
    for i in range(n):
        if parent[i] == -1:
            if root != -1:
                return False
            root = i

    return root != -1


```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py

def validateBinaryTreeNodes(n, leftChild, rightChild):
    parent = [-1] * n
    for i in range(n):
        if leftChild[i] != -1:
            if parent[leftChild[i]] != -1:
                return False
            parent[leftChild[i]] = i
        if rightChild[i] != -1:
            if parent[rightChild[i]] != -1:
                return False
            parent[rightChild[i]] = i
    
    root = -1
    for i in range(n):
        if parent[i] == -1:
            if root != -1:
                return False
            root = i

    return root != -1


```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py

def validateBinaryTreeNodes(n, leftChild, rightChild):
    parent = [-1] * n
    for i in range(n):
        if leftChild[i] != -1:
            if parent[leftChild[i]] != -1:
                return False
            parent[leftChild[i]] = i
        if rightChild[i] != -1:
            if parent[rightChild[i]] != -1:
                return False
            parent[rightChild[i]] = i
    
    root = -1
    for i in range(n):
        if parent[i] == -1:
            if root != -1:
                return False
            root = i

    return root != -1


```

## Test Case 5

### Modified Program

```py

def validateBinaryTreeNodes(n, leftChild, rightChild):
    parent = [-1] * n
    for i in range(n):
        if leftChild[i] != -1:
            if parent[leftChild[i]] != -1:
                return False
            parent[leftChild[i]] = i
        if rightChild[i] != -1:
            if parent[rightChild[i]] != -1:
                return False
            parent[rightChild[i]] = i
    
    root = -1
    for i in range(n):
        if parent[i] == -1:
            if root != -1:
                return False
            root = i

    return root != -1


```

## Test Case 6

### Modified Program

```py

def validateBinaryTreeNodes(n, leftChild, rightChild):
    parent = [-1] * n
    for i in range(n):
        if leftChild[i] != -1:
            if parent[leftChild[i]] != -1:
                return False
            parent[leftChild[i]] = i
        if rightChild[i] != -1:
            if parent[rightChild[i]] != -1:
                return False
            parent[rightChild[i]] = i
    
    root = -1
    for i in range(n):
        if parent[i] == -1:
            if root != -1:
                return False
            root = i

    return root != -1


```

## Test Case 7

### Modified Program

```py

def validateBinaryTreeNodes(n, leftChild, rightChild):
    parent = [-1] * n
    for i in range(n):
        if leftChild[i] != -1:
            if parent[leftChild[i]] != -1:
                return False
            parent[leftChild[i]] = i
        if rightChild[i] != -1:
            if parent[rightChild[i]] != -1:
                return False
            parent[rightChild[i]] = i
    
    root = -1
    for i in range(n):
        if parent[i] == -1:
            if root != -1:
                return False
            root = i

    return root != -1


```

## Test Case 8

### Modified Program

```py

def validateBinaryTreeNodes(n, leftChild, rightChild):
    parent = [-1] * n
    for i in range(n):
        if leftChild[i] != -1:
            if parent[leftChild[i]] != -1:
                return False
            parent[leftChild[i]] = i
        if rightChild[i] != -1:
            if parent[rightChild[i]] != -1:
                return False
            parent[rightChild[i]] = i
    
    root = -1
    for i in range(n):
        if parent[i] == -1:
            if root != -1:
                return False
            root = i

    return root != -1


```

## Test Case 9

### Modified Program

```py

def validateBinaryTreeNodes(n, leftChild, rightChild):
    parent = [-1] * n
    for i in range(n):
        if leftChild[i] != -1:
            if parent[leftChild[i]] != -1:
                return False
            parent[leftChild[i]] = i
        if rightChild[i] != -1:
            if parent[rightChild[i]] != -1:
                return False
            parent[rightChild[i]] = i
    
    root = -1
    for i in range(n):
        if parent[i] == -1:
            if root != -1:
                return False
            root = i

    return root != -1


```

## Test Case 10

### Modified Program

```py

def validateBinaryTreeNodes(n, leftChild, rightChild):
    parent = [-1] * n
    for i in range(n):
        if leftChild[i] != -1:
            if parent[leftChild[i]] != -1:
                return False
            parent[leftChild[i]] = i
        if rightChild[i] != -1:
            if parent[rightChild[i]] != -1:
                return False
            parent[rightChild[i]] = i
    
    root = -1
    for i in range(n):
        if parent[i] == -1:
            if root != -1:
                return False
            root = i

    return root != -1


```
